The credit freeze locks the data at the consumer reporting agency until an individual gives permission for the release of the data.\r\n\r\n# Lesson 4: Acquiring and understanding credit reports and credit scores - Consumers can typically check their credit history by requesting credit reports from credit agencies and demanding correction of information if necessary.\r\nIn the US, the Fair Credit Reporting Act governs businesses that compile credit reports. The consumer credit reporting agencies it governs provide a free copy of the credit reports for any consumer who requests it, once per year.\r\n\r\n# Lesson 5: free credit monitoring and credit tracker - Credit report monitoring or credit tracking is the monitoring of one’s credit history in order to detect any suspicious activity or changes.
